title="\xc5\xbdeljko Ivanek">\xc5\xbdeljko Ivanek</a>\n</th>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td><img alt="Yes" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Black_x.svg/16px-Black_x.svg.png" title="X mark" width="16" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Black_x.svg/24px-Black_x.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Black_x.svg/32px-Black_x.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="600" /><span style="display:none;">N</span></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td><img alt="Yes" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Black_x.svg/16px-Black_x.svg.png" title="X mark" width="16" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Black_x.svg/24px-Black_x.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Black_x.svg/32px-Black_x.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="600" /><span style="display:none;">N</span></td>\n<td><img alt="Yes" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Black_x.svg/16px-Black_x.svg.png" title="X mark" width="16" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Black_x.svg/24px-Black_x.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Black_x.svg/32px-Black_x.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="600" /><span style="display:none;">N</span></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td></td>\n<td>3\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n</div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Accolades">Accolades</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ridley_Scott&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Accolades">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ridley_Scott_at_the_RCA_July_2015.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Ridley_Scott_at_the_RCA_July_2015.jpg/220px-Ridley_Scott_at_the_RCA_July_2015.jpg" width="220" height="264" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Ridley_Scott_at_the_RCA_July_2015.jpg/330px-Ridley_Scott_at_the_RCA_July_2015.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Ridley_Scott_at_the_RCA_July_2015.jpg/440px-Ridley_Scott_at_the_RCA_July_2015.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2255" data-file-height="2703" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ridley_Scott_at_the_RCA_July_2015.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Sir Ridley Scott, Honorary Doctor, at the <a href="/wiki/Royal_College_of_Art" title="Royal College of Art">Royal College of Art</a>, July 2015</div></div></div>\n<p>Scott was appointed <a href="/wiki/Knight_Bachelor" title="Knight Bachelor">Knight Bachelor</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2003_New_Year_Honours" title="2003 New Year Honours">2003 New Year Honours</a> for services to the British film industry.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> He received his accolade from <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_II" title="Elizabeth II">Queen Elizabeth II</a> at a investiture ceremony at <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Palace" title="Buckingham Palace">Buckingham Palace</a> on 8 July 2003.<sup id="cite_ref-knighted_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-knighted-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Scott admitted feeling "stunned and truly humbled" after the ceremony, saying, "As a boy growing up in <a href="/wiki/South_Shields" title="South Shields">South Shields</a>, I could never have imagined that I would receive such a special recognition. I am truly humbled to receive this treasured award and believe it also further recognises the excellence of the British film industry."<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>He has been nominated for three <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Directing" class="mw-redirect" title="Academy Award for Directing">Academy Awards for Directing</a>\xe2\x80\x94<i>Thelma &amp; Louise</i>, <i>Gladiator</i> and <i>Black Hawk Down</i>\xe2\x80\x94as well as a Golden Globe, BAFTA and 2 <a href="/wiki/Primetime_Emmy_Award" title="Primetime Emmy Award">Primetime Emmy Awards</a>. In 1995, Ridley and his brother <a href="/wiki/Tony_Scott" title="Tony Scott">Tony</a> received the <a href="/wiki/BAFTA_Award" class="mw-redirect" title="BAFTA Award">BAFTA</a> for <a href="/wiki/BAFTA_Outstanding_British_Contribution_to_Cinema_Award" title="BAFTA Outstanding British Contribution to Cinema Award">Outstanding British Contribution To Cinema</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Outstanding_contribution_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Outstanding_contribution-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> In 2018 he received the highest accolade from BAFTA, the <a href="/wiki/BAFTA_Fellowship" title="BAFTA Fellowship">BAFTA Fellowship</a>, for lifetime achievement.<sup id="cite_ref-BAFTA_Felowship_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BAFTA_Felowship-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Scott was inducted into the <a href="/wiki/EMP_Museum#Science_Fiction_Hall_of_Fame" class="mw-redirect" title="EMP Museum">Science Fiction Hall of Fame</a> in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-hof2007_130-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hof2007-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> In 2017 the German newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/Frankfurter_Allgemeine_Zeitung" title="Frankfurter Allgemeine Zeitung">FAZ</a></i> compared Scott\'s influence on the science fiction film genre to Sir <a href="/wiki/Alfred_Hitchcock" title="Alfred Hitchcock">Alfred Hitchcock</a>\'s on <a href="/wiki/Thriller_film" title="Thriller film">thrillers</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_Ford" title="John Ford">John Ford</a>\'s on <a href="/wiki/Western_(genre)" title="Western (genre)">Westerns</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> In 2011, he received a star on the <a href="/wiki/Hollywood_Walk_of_Fame" title="Hollywood Walk of Fame">Hollywood Walk of Fame</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2012, Scott was among the <a href="/wiki/Culture_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Culture of the United Kingdom">British cultural icons</a> selected by artist Sir <a href="/wiki/Peter_Blake_(artist)" title="Peter Blake (artist)">Peter Blake</a> to appear in a new version of his most famous artwork \xe2\x80\x93 the Beatles\' <i><a href="/wiki/Sgt._Pepper%27s_Lonely_Hearts_Club_Band" title="Sgt. Pepper&#39;s Lonely Hearts Club Band">Sgt. Pepper\'s Lonely Hearts Club Band</a></i> album cover \xe2\x80\x93 to celebrate the British cultural figures of his life that he most admires to mark his 80th birthday.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> On 3 July 2015, he was awarded an honorary doctorate by the <a href="/wiki/Royal_College_of_Art" title="Royal College of Art">Royal College of Art</a> in a ceremony at the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Albert_Hall" title="Royal Albert Hall">Royal Albert Hall</a> in London at which he described how he still keeps on his office wall his school report placing him 31st out of 31 in his class, and how his teacher encouraged him to pursue what became his passion at art school.<sup id="cite_ref-RCA_134-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RCA-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<table
